<h1 _ngcontent-gcx-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.calendarManager (日程管理能力)"> @ohos.calendarManager (日程管理能力) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-gcx-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块提供日历与日程管理能力，包括日历和日程的创建、删除、修改、查询等。</p>    <ul>     <li>      <p>日历管理器<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendarmanager">CalendarManager</a>用于管理日历<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendar">Calendar</a>。</p></li>     <li>      <p>日历<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendar">Calendar</a>主要包含账户信息<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendaraccount">CalendarAccount</a>和配置信息<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendarconfig">CalendarConfig</a>。日历Calendar与日程Event属于从属关系，需要先创建日历Calendar对象，然后再通过日历Calendar创建日程Event对象，一个Calendar可以有多个Event，一个Event只属于一个Calendar。日历管理器是对日历的管理，日程过滤器是对日程的管理。</p></li>    </ul>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <ul>       <li>        <p>本模块首批接口从API version 10开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p></li>       <li>        <p>进行日历或日程的读取时，需要申请ohos.permission.READ_CALENDAR或ohos.permission.READ_WHOLE_CALENDAR权限。</p></li>       <li>        <p>进行日历或日程的添加、删除或修改时，需要申请ohos.permission.WRITE_CALENDAR或ohos.permission.WRITE_WHOLE_CALENDAR权限。</p></li>      </ul>     </div></div></div>    <p>申请对应权限之后，支持的相关操作可见下表。</p>    <div class="tablenoborder">     <div class="tbBox"><table>      <thead>       <tr>        <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">申请的权限</th>        <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">支持的日历账户操作范围</th>        <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">支持的日程操作范围</th>       </tr>      </thead>             <tbody><tr>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ohos.permission.READ_CALENDAR</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">         <p>- 读取系统默认日历账户</p>         <p>- 读取当前应用创建的日历账户</p></td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">         <p>- 读取系统默认日历账户下当前应用创建的日程</p>         <p>- 读取当前应用创建的日历账户下当前应用创建的日程</p></td>       </tr>       <tr>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ohos.permission.WRITE_CALENDAR</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">- 添加、删除或修改当前应用创建的日历账户</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">         <p>- 添加、删除或修改系统默认日历账户下当前应用创建的日程</p>         <p>- 添加、删除或修改当前应用创建的日历账户下当前应用创建的日程</p></td>       </tr>       <tr>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ohos.permission.READ_WHOLE_CALENDAR</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">- 读取所有日历账户</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">- 读取所有应用创建的日程</td>       </tr>       <tr>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">ohos.permission.WRITE_WHOLE_CALENDAR</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">- 添加、删除或修改所有日历账户</td>        <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">- 添加、删除或修改所有应用创建的日程</td>       </tr>           </tbody></table></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div id="calendarmanagergetcalendarmanager" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">calendarManager.getCalendarManager<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="calendarmanagergetcalendarmanager" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getCalendarManager(context: Context): CalendarManager</p>     <p>根据上下文获取CalendarManager对象，用于管理日历。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>： SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>     <p><strong>模型约束</strong>：此接口仅可在Stage模型下使用。</p>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">Context</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">应用上下文Context，Stage模型的应用Context定义见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-application-uiabilitycontext">Context</a>。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.10.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.10.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">CalendarManager</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">返回创建的CalendarManager对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例</strong>：</p>     <div _ngcontent-gcx-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-gcx-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">CalendarManager<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="calendarmanager" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>下列API示例中需先通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendarmanagergetcalendarmanager">getCalendarManager()</a>方法获取CalendarManager对象，再通过此对象调用对应方法，进行Calendar的创建、删除、修改、查询等操作。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>： SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1564px;">     <h3 id="createcalendar" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">createCalendar<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="createcalendar" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>createCalendar(calendarAccount: CalendarAccount, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;Calendar&gt;): void</p>     <p>根据日历账户信息，创建一个Calendar对象，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>需要权限</strong>：API version 21之前，使用此接口需申请ohos.permission.WRITE_CALENDAR权限；</p>     <p>从API version 21开始，使用此接口需申请ohos.permission.WRITE_CALENDAR或ohos.permission.WRITE_WHOLE_CALENDAR。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>： SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.8.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">calendarAccount</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendaraccount">CalendarAccount</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">日历账户信息。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">AsyncCallback&lt;<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#calendar">Calendar</a>&gt;</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数，返回创建的Calendar对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码详细介绍请参考<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-universal">通用错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.11.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.9.11.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">201</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Permission denied.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="editevent12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span <p>通过跳转到日程创建页面创建单个日程，入参Event不填日程id，使用Promise异步回调。使用该接口创建的日程，系统日历可以进行查询和修改，申请到READ_WHOLE_CALENDAR权限的三方应用可以查询，申请到WRITE_WHOLE_CALENDAR权限的三方应用可以修改。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>： SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>     <p><strong>参数</strong>：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table> width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.18.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">event</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#event">Event</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">Promise对象，返回日程的id，日程id是日程的唯一标识符，是数据库的自增主键。创建失败时没有返回值；当返回值小于0时代表用户取消创建；当返回值大于0时代表日程创建成功；没有等于0的情况。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 254px;">     <h2 id="calendar" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">Calendar<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="calendar" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>下列API示例中需先通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#createcalendar">createCalendar()</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#getcalendar">getCalendar()</a>中任一方法获取Calendar对象，再通过此对象调用对应方法，对该Calendar下的日程进行创建、删除、修改、查询等操作。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>： SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 477px;">     <h3 id="属性" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" <p>根据日程id，批量删除日程，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 21开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>： SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p> </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 278px;">     <h2 id="eventfilter" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">EventFilter<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="eventfilter" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>日程过滤器，查询日程时进行筛选过滤，获取符合条件的日程。</p>     <p>通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#filterbyid">filterById()</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#filterbytime">filterByTime()</a>、<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#filterbytitle">filterByTitle()</a>任一方法获取日程过滤器，传入<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#getevents">getEvents()</a>过滤。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>： SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1769px;">     <h3 id="filterbyid" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">filterById<i class="anchor-icon class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>static filterById(ids: number[]): EventFilter</p>     <p>根据日程id过滤日程。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ids</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">number[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1449px;">     <h3 id="filterbytitle" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">filterByTitle<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 522px;">     <h2 id="eventtype" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">EventType<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>日程类型枚举。</p>     <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.5.1.4.1.1" width="33.33333333333333%">名称</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.5.1.4.1.2" width="33.33333333333333%">值</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.48.5.1.4.1.3" width="33.33333333333333%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">NORMAL</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">0</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">普通日程，例如会议，闹钟等日常提醒的日程。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">IMPORTANT</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">1</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="33.33333333333333%">重要日程，例如结婚纪念日等具有重要意义的日期，不推荐三方开发者使用，重要日程类型不支持一键服务跳转功能及无法自定义提醒时间。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>重复日程重复规则。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力</strong>：SystemCapability.Applications.CalendarData</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.49.4.1.6.1.1" width="20%">名称</th>         <th align="left"   <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">recurrenceFrequency</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-calendarmanager#recurrencefrequency">RecurrenceFrequency</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>日程重复规则类型。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">expire</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>重复周期截止日。格式为13位时间戳，不填时则日程无截止日期。</p>          <p>当expire与count和interval同时设置时，以先到达的限制条件及效果为准。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 11开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">count<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>重复日程的重复次数，取值为非负整数，浮点数输入将向下取整，不填时默认为0，表示不会限定重复次数，会一直重复。取值为负时，效果等同于取值为0。</p>          <p>当count与interval和expire同时设置时，以先到达的限制条件及效果为准。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">interval<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>重复日程的重复周期，取值为非负整数，浮点数输入将向下取整。</p>          <p>不填时默认为0，当取值为0、1或负值时，表示日程每天/周/月/年重复一次。</p>          <p>当interval与count和expire同时设置时，以先到达的限制条件及效果为准。</p>          <p>此属性与recurrenceFrequency重复规则相关，不同的重复规则下，表示的重复周期不同，以interval取2为例，分为以下几种情况：</p>          <p>每天重复时：表示日程每两天重复一次。</p>          <p>每周重复时：表示日程每两周重复一次。</p>          <p>每月重复时：表示日程每两月重复一次。</p>          <p>每年重复时：表示日程每两年重复一次。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">excludedDates<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>重复日程的排除日期，参数取值为时间戳格式，不填时，默认为空，表示没有排除的日期，0或负数为无效值，与空值效果相同。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">daysOfWeek<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>按照一周第几天重复。不填时，默认为空，表示没有一周第几天重复的规则。范围为1到7，对应周一到周日，其他值为无效值，与空值效果相同。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">daysOfMonth<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>按照一个月第几天重复。不填时，默认为空，表示没有一个月第几天重复的规则。范围为1到31，1到31对应1到31号，其他值为无效值，与空值效果相同。若当月没有29号、30号或31号，则29、30、31也为无效值。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">daysOfYear<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>按照一年第几天重复。不填时，默认为空，表示没有一年第几天重复的规则。范围为1到366，1到366表示一年的1到366天，其他值为无效值，与空值效果相同。若当年没有366天，366也为无效值。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">weeksOfMonth<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">number[]</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">          <p>按照一个月第几周重复。不填时，默认为空，表示没有一个月第几周重复的规则。范围为1到5，1到5为每月的第1到第5周，其他值为无效值，与空值效果相同。若当月没有第五周，5也为无效值。</p>          <p><strong>元服务API：</strong> 从API version 12开始，该接口支持在元服务中使用。</p></td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="20%">weeksOfYear<sup>12+</sup></td>         <td
